				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Judas Maccabaeus, HWV 63 (Handel, George Frideric)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 acts
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1746 (Act I: 8/9 July - 22 July; remainder completed 11 August)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Judas Maccabaeus
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="es">Judas Maccabeus</span>; <span title="ja">ユダス・マカベウス</span>; <span title="pl">Juda Machabeusz</span>; <span title="he">יהודה המכבי (הנדל)</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/174965030">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Judas_Maccabaeus_(Handel)">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/174965030">174965030</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_of_Congress_Control_Number" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Library of Congress Control Number">LCCN</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://id.loc.gov/authorities/names/n82159318">n82159318</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300064837">300064837</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb13913109f">13913109f</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Handel,_George_Frideric" title="Category:Handel, George Frideric">Handel, George Frideric</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>HWV 63
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IGH 228
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 acts:
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act I
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Overture 
</dd><dd>2. Chorus: Mourn, ye afflicted children 
</dd><dd>3. Duet: From this dread scene (Israelitish Man, Israelitish Woman)
</dd><dd>4. Chorus: For Sion lamentation make
</dd><dd>5. Recitative: Not vain is all this storm of grief (Simon)
</dd><dd>6. Aria: Pious orgies, pious airs (Simon)
</dd><dd>7. Chorus: O Father, whose almighty pow'r 
</dd><dd>8. Recitative: I feel the Deity within (Simon)
</dd><dd>9. Aria and Chorus: Arm, arm, ye brave (Simon) 
</dd><dd>10. Recitative: 'Tis well, my friends! (Judas Maccabaeus)
</dd><dd>11. Aria and Chorus
<dl><dd>a. Aria: Call forth thy pow'rs, my soul (Judas Maccabaeus) 
</dd><dd>b. Chorus: Lead on, lead on!
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>12. Recitative: To Heav'n's almighty King we kneel (Israelitish woman) 
</dd><dd>13. Air and Duet
<dl><dd>a. Air: O liberty, thou choicest treasure (Israelitish woman)
</dd><dd>b. Duet: Come ever-smiling liberty (Israelitish Woman, Israelitish Man)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>14. Recitative: My zealous father, now at rest (Judas Maccabaeus)
</dd><dd>15. Trio and Chorus: Disdainful of danger
<dl><dd>(Priest, Judas Maccabaeus, Simon; Israelitish Woman)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>16. Recitative: Haste ye, my brethren (Simon) 
</dd><dd>17. Chorus: Hear us, O Lord 
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act II
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>18. Chorus: Fall'n is the foe 
</dd><dd>19. Duet and Chorus: Sion now her head shall raise (Israelitish Woman and Man) 
</dd><dd>20. Recitative: Oh, let eternal honours (Israelitish Woman)
</dd><dd>21. Aria: From mighty kings he took the spoil (Israelitish Woman) 
</dd><dd>22. Chorus: Hail, Judea, happy land
</dd><dd>23. Recitative: Thanks to my brethren! (Judas Maccabaeus)
</dd><dd>24. Aria: How vain is man (Judas Maccabaeus) 
</dd><dd>25. Recitative: Oh Judas, oh my brethren (Israelitish Messenger) 
</dd><dd>26. Aria and Chorus: Ah! wretched, wretched Israel (Israelitish Woman) 
</dd><dd>27. Recitative: My arms! (Judas Maccabaeus) 
</dd><dd>28. Aria and Chorus: Sound an alarm! (Judas Maccabaeus) 
</dd><dd>29. Recitative: Enough! To Heav'n we leave the rest! (Simon) 
</dd><dd>30. Chorus: We never will bow down 
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act III
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>31. Aria: Father of Heav'n (Priest) 
</dd><dd>32. Recitative: Oh grant it, Heav'n (Israelitish Woman) 
</dd><dd>33. Aria: So shall the lute and harp awake (Israelitish Woman) 
</dd><dd>34. Recitative: From Capharsalama on eagle wings I fly (Israelitish Messenger) 
</dd><dd>35. Chorus: See, the conqu'ring hero comes! 
</dd><dd>36. March 
</dd><dd>37. Chorus: Sing unto God 
</dd><dd>38. Recitative: Sweet flow the strains (Judas Maccabaeus) 
</dd><dd>39. Aria: No unhallowed desire (Judas Maccabaeus) 
</dd><dd>40. Duet: Oh lovely peace (Israelitish Woman, Israelitish Man) 
</dd><dd>41. Aria and Chorus: Rejoice, oh Judah! (Simon)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1746 (Act I: 8/9 July - 22 July; remainder completed 11 August)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1747-04-01 in London, Covent Garden.
<dl><dd>Soli, Chorus and Orchestra, George Frideric Handel (conductor)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Morell,_Thomas" title="Category:Morell, Thomas">Thomas Morell</a> (1703-1784), revised
<dl><dd>from the 1st book of "Maccabees" from the Apocrypha and a few details from Josephus' "Antiquitates Judaicae". This work represents Morell's first collaboration with Handel.
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>English
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque" title="Category:Baroque">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>voices, chorus, orchestra <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd><i>Roles</i>
<dl><dd>Judas Maccabaeus (tenor)<br />Simon, his Brother (bass)<br />Israelite Woman (soprano)<br />Israelite Man (mezzo-soprano)<br />Eupolemus, the Jewish Ambassador to Rome (alto)<br />First Messenger (alto)<br />Second Messenger (bass)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Mixed Chorus</i> (SATB)
<dl><dd>Israelites, Youths, Virgins
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Orchestra</i> 
<dl><dd>2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 bassoons<br />2 horns (F/G), 3 trumpets (D), timpani, organ, strings </div>
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
